<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-07f81ff" data-v="4" data-block-id="07f81ff"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-07f81ff-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-07f81ff-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-51e1ed1" id="what-sets-our-pop-workplace-preschool-in-ngee-ann-polytechnic-apart" data-block-id="51e1ed1"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">What Sets our POP Workplace Preschool in Ngee Ann Polytechnic Apart</h2></div>



<p>The<a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener"> Little Skool-House </a>preschool in Clementi Road is located at Ngee Ann Polytechnic. Our <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">award-winning educators</a> foster a supportive learning environment and offer daily opportunities to play and develop in optimal health and academic excellence.</p>



<p>Being the <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">chosen preschool by top institutions</a>, our POP Workplace kindergarten in Ngee Ann Polytechnic is the preferred infant care centre for employees of our workplace partner in Clementi Road. Established to provide working parents with child and infant care services during working hours, it is a convenient option for working parents in the area.</p>
</div></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-14e19f2" id="programmes-offered" data-block-id="14e19f2"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Programmes Offered</h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-57bd5c0" data-block-id="57bd5c0"><p class="stk-block-text__text">We run a full-day infant care programme and a choice of full-day and half-day preschool programmes in which our educators follow a comprehensive <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/curriculum/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">curriculum</a> that has led to 93% of Little Skool-House children being <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/our-difference/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Highly Proficient in both English and Mandarin</a>. We also offer a range of <a href="https://www.littleskoolhouse.com/curriculum/enrichment-programmes/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">enrichment programmes</a> that supplement the holistic development of your child.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-subtitle stk-block-subtitle stk-block stk-aa9bae1" data-block-id="aa9bae1"><p class="stk-block-subtitle__text stk-subtitle has-text-color has-text-align-left">Principal</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-subtitle stk-block-subtitle stk-block stk-26fdf9c" data-block-id="26fdf9c"><p class="stk-block-subtitle__text stk-subtitle has-text-color has-text-align-left">Master of Science in Early Childhood Education (M.SC. in ECE)</p></div>
</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-f17e6ac" data-block-id="f17e6ac"><p class="stk-block-text__text">Dr. Seuss once wrote: “The more that you read, the more things you will know. The more that you learn, the more places you’ll go.” Yvonne has put this into practice by teaching the little ones how words can make stories, encouraging them to use their imagination to create characters, and helping them develop a love for books.</p></div>

                                <p class="stk-block-text__text"><!-- wp:paragraph -->
</p><p>Governed by ECDA, the Partner Operator (POP) scheme supports appointed centres to improve the accessibility, affordability and quality of childcare and infant care services. Rest assured that our programmes and curriculum are the same across all Little Skool-House centres.</p>
<!-- /wp:paragraph -->

<!-- wp:paragraph -->
<p>Within the Little Skool-House network of centres, 14 of them operate as Partner Operator (POP) centres under the Partner Operator scheme governed by ECDA. This programme aims to improve accessibility, affordability and quality of childcare and infant care services for working parents. 12 of these centres operate on the premises of our partner employer. However, in all other aspects, our POP centres are consistent with all other Little Skool-House centres in the delivery of programmes and curriculum.</p>
